              <div class="slides-text-info-block1 block-left slides-text-light" style="top: 35%; width: 57%; transform: translateX(4%);">
                <p class="slides-text18 slides-text-dark">"When I moved to Stroud in January 1997, Stroud Valleys Artspace was in its infancy. I’d left a studio in a semi-derelict warehouse in Lancaster, and found a studio in what was then a semi-derelict warehouse in John Street where I joined an eclectic group of artists who became the core of Stroud Open Studios.</p>
                <p class="slides-text18 slides-text-dark">Artists opening their doors and inviting you into their working spaces, seeing where and how people work, and connecting the art with the people who make it is what sustains this wonderful annual event. It also enables you to buy pieces direct from the artist.</p>
                <p class="slides-text18 slides-text-dark">The Taster Exhibition, with examples of work by every artist, enables you to choose where to go, and who to see; from experience it’s impossible to visit them all!</p>
                <p class="slides-text18 slides-text-dark">This year, following major surgery, my studio will not be open so I will visit studios I’ve long wanted to see. I hope to bump into you along the way!"</p>
                <p class="slides-text18 slides-text-dark" style="font-style: italic;">Chris Bingle, artist.</p>
              </div>
            </div>
            </div>
            
            <div class="slides-right  no-select">
              <div class="logo" style="top: 7.5%; left: 86.5%; width: 45%; height: 45%; position: absolute;">
                <svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg">
                  <!--<image xlink:href="/logo2.svg" width="85%" height="85%" z-index="1"/>-->
                  <span class="logo2"/>
                </svg>
              </div>
              <img class="img9" style="height: 45%; top: 47.5%; left: 10%; width: 80%;" src="/placeholder.jpg" data-src="/MayDarbyshire.jpg">
              <p class="slides-text5-1" style="top: 93%;">May Darbyshire, Artist in Residence at SVA</p>
            </div>

              <p class="slides-text3 slides-text-dark">SVA provides artist studio spaces and an artistic programme. SVA was set up in 1996 by artists for artists. The first Open Studios was held 6 weeks after moving into the building.</p>
              <p class="slides-text3 slides-text-dark">SVA presents a year round programme of exhibitions and events in John Street and the Brunel Goods shed.</p>

              <p class="slides-text1 slides-text-dark">Three Storeys</p>
              <p class="slides-text2 slides-text-dark">Nailsworth</p>
                  <a class="slides-text2 slides-text8" href="https://www.threestoreys.co.uk/" target="_blank">
                    <span class="slides-text-dark slides-text8">threestoreys.co.uk</span>
                  </a>
              <p class="slides-text3 slides-text-dark">A multi-functional creative venue in the heart of Nailsworth, Gloucestershire – a unique community for working together.</p>
              <p class="slides-text3 slides-text-dark">A long refurbishment programme uncovered layers of history in the process. Some of the building may date back to the start of Nailsworth Brewery around 1820.</p>

            <div class="slides-left no-select slide-color">
              <p class="slides-text1 slides-text-dark">Piccadilly Mill</p>
              <p class="slides-text2 slides-text-dark">Lower St, Stroud</p>
              <p class="slides-text3 slides-text-dark">Piccadilly Mill is a large industrial former mill, dating from the 19th century. It is constructed of red brick with yellow brick detailing in the form of Voussoirs over the windows.</p>
              <p class="slides-text3 slides-text-dark">Though large, it is well hidden from any significant view by virtue of its location surrounded by the houses and cottages in Middle Street and Lower Street. It is used by a variety of local artists and businesses.</p>

                      </svg>

                </a>
                <p class="slides-text9">Earthy and textural stoneware vessels celebrating the natural clay , shape and form.</p>
                <p class="slides-text9" style="font-style: italic;">The sat nav should take you to my village green , park there and walk down the hill and turn right</p>

            <div class="numbertext">42 / 51</div>

            <div class="slides-head">
            <p class="slides-text15">BITE</p>
            <p class="slides-text15">An exhibition showcasing four selected artists from Bristol alongside SITE festival</p>
            </div>

            <div class="slides-left  no-select">
              <div class="slides-text-info-block1 block-left1 slides-text-light">
                <p class="slides-text16">10th-24th June</p>
                <p class="slides-text16">Saturday & Sundays 11am-6pm</p>
                <p class="slides-text16">Wednesdays - Fridays 10am-3pm</p>
                <p class="slides-text16">SVA John St Gallery, 4 John St,</p>
                <p class="slides-text16">Stroud, GL5 2HA</p>

                <p class="slides-text9">Bristol is a city with a reputation for being a hub for artists. The ever evolving artist networks often spring from the communities formed in artist studios. Showing alongside SITE Festival, this exhibition spotlights artists from across four of the major studio spaces in Bristol.</p>
                <p class="slides-text9">Across from an inner city farm is BV studios, an anonymous looking building from the outside, previously a printing works and home to over 100 artists and makers.</p>

              </div>
            </div>

            <div class="slides-middle no-select">
              <img class="img5" src="/placeholder.jpg" data-src="/adam-hedley.jpg">
              <div class="slides-text-info-block1 block-middle slides-text-light" style="top: 25.5%;">
                <p class="slides-text9" style="margin: 0 0">Adam Hedley, who works from a space at BV, makes mesmorising abstract paintings. He works slowly and methodically to create immersive paintings that have a hypnotising quality.</p>

              </div>
        
            </div>
            
            <div class="slides-right  no-select">
              <img class="img6" src="/placeholder.jpg" data-src="/BoeleKeimer.jpg">

              <div class="slides-text-info-block1 block-right slides-text-light" style="top: 41%; width: 25%; height: 50%">

                <p class="slides-text9">Vera Boele-Keimer’s minimal work sits in contrast to the chaotic mayhem of Stokes Croft where the longstanding Jamaica Street studios, one of the largest artist- led studios outside of London, is based. The studios huge windows look out onto a busy crossroads of music venues, pubs and massage parlours. Vera’s work explores the boundaries of painting, drawing and sculpture.</p>

              </div>
            
            </div>
            
              <svg class="lines line7">
                <rect class="lines-rect lines-rect2 neutral-line" x="3%" y="70%" width="27.6%"/>
              </svg>
              <svg class="lines line7">
                <rect class="lines-rect lines-rect2 neutral-line" x="69.65%" y="70%" width="27.6%"/>
              </svg>


              <p class="slides-text5" style="top: 93%; left:34%;">Adam Hedley</p>
              <p class="slides-text5" style="top: 33%; left:96.75%;">Vera Boele-Keimer</p>

          </div>



          <!-- SLIDE 42 -->
          <div class="mySlides fade">
            <div class="numbertext">43 / 51</div>

            <div class="slides-left no-select">
              <img class="img8" src="/placeholder.jpg" data-src="/Ptaszkowska+K.Moon+Mother+Be+Cool.jpg">
              <div class="slides-text-info-block1 block-left1 slides-text-light" style="top: 6%;">
                <p class="slides-text9">Karolina Ptaszkowska’s studio is based at St Anne’s House, also known as Bricks, a multi use space and a hub for artists as well as social enterprises. Karolina draws from a multitude of sources including mythology and psychology to create dreamlike paintings that transport you to an unseen world.</p>

              </div>
            </div>

            <div class="slides-middle no-select">
              <div class="slides-text-info-block1 block-middle1 slides-text-light" style="top: 6%;">
                <p class="slides-text9">Mahali O’Hare works from her space at the internationally renowned Spike Island which is a former tea packing warehouse and situated between the River Avon and the Harbourside. Mahali’s impactful paintings shift between the figurative and landscape and are rooted in the tradition of still life.</p>

              </div>
        
            </div>
            
            <div class="slides-right  no-select">
              <img class="img7" src="/placeholder.jpg" data-src="/Mahali o_hare Solitude-Oil-on-canvas-20-x-20-cm-2021.jpg">

                <p class="slides-text9">By bringing a selection of exciting artists from Bristol to Stroud during SITE Festival and drawing attention to the dynamic and fluid artist communities in Bristol, we hope to encourage the potential for collaboration and cross- pollination of ideas. This exhibition has been selected by Mary Roberts-Holmes and Jo Leahy.</p>

              </div>

            <div class="numbertext">44 / 51</div>

            <div class="slides-head" style="transform: translate(54%,10%)">
            <p class="slides-text15">In memory of Adam White</p>
            <p class="slides-text15">a retrospective Open Studio</p>
            </div>

            <div class="slides-left  no-select">
              <img class="img9" style="height: 35%; top: 0%; left: 0%;" src="/placeholder.jpg" data-src="/Adam White 01. Photo credit Brendan Francis.JPG">
              <img class="img9" style="height: 65%; top: 0%; left: 0%;" src="/placeholder.jpg" data-src="/adam-white.jpg">
              <p class="slides-text5" style="top: 85%; left:33.75%;">Adam White</p>
            </div>

            <div class="slides-middle no-select">

              <div class="slides-text-info-block1 block-middle slides-text-light" style="top: 23%; height: 70%; width: 26%; transform: translateX(7%);">
                <p class="slides-text16">10th-11th & 17th-18th June</p>
                <p class="slides-text16">Sat & Sun 11am-6pm</p>
                <p class="slides-text16">SVA, 4 John St, Stroud, GL5 2HA</p>
                <a class="slides-text8" href="https://www.adamwhiteartist.co.uk/" target="_blank">
                  <span class="slides-text16">www.adamwhiteartist.co.uk</span>
                </a>
                <p class="slides-text9">Adam White wanted as many people as possible to continue to enjoy his wonderful work so his studio will be open for Site Festival and much of his musings can still be found on his website. Adam has been making art with SVA since the humble beginnings of our organisation, and there are few words to describe him in his entirety. So here are a few of Adam’s own words to give an insight into his passion for art.</p>
                <p class="slides-text9" style="font-style: italic;">“I don’t see myself as an artist in the modern sense. I just make stuff. My work is more informed by archaeology and natural history and life than the contemporary art</p>

              </div>
              
            </div>
            
            <div class="slides-right  no-select">

              <div class="slides-text-info-block1 block-right slides-text-light" style="top: 23%; width: 26%; transform: translateX(-5.5%); height: 70%">
                <p class="slides-text9"  style="font-style: italic; margin: 0 0!important;">market. I ’d be happy if you left me alone for a month in Chauvet cave with an oily ferruginous stick and working with the cave paintings... in my mind adding eight-legged mammoths.</p>
                <br>
                <p class="slides-text9"  style="font-style: italic; margin: 0 0!important;">I no longer believe that beauty is a societal construct or some vestigial remnant of a biological urge. Archaeology, history and politics also inform my work as does life. I ’ve been decisively blessed by soul-cleaving illness since I was a boy and have faced extinction more than one might politely expect before breakfast. This compels an urgency in my work. Any personal circumstances I mine and try to make universal. The work is about you.”</p>
                <p class="slides-text9"  style="font-style: italic; margin: 10% 0!important;">Adam passed away on 25.12.22 aged 54.</p>

              </div>
            
            </div>
            
              <svg class="lines line7">
                <rect class="lines-rect lines-rect2 neutral-line" x="38%" y="70%" width="57%"/>
              </svg>
          </div>

            <div class="slides-head" style="transform: translate(-1%,10%)">
            <p class="slides-text15">The Studios Collective</p>
            </div>

            <div class="slides-left no-select">

              <div class="slides-text-info-block1 block-left slides-text-light" style="top: 21.5%; height: 30%; width: 26%; transform: translateX(9%);">
                <p class="slides-text16">10th-11th & 17th-18th June</p>
                <p class="slides-text16">Sat & Sun 11am-6pm</p>
                <p class="slides-text16">Stroud Pottery</p>
                <p class="slides-text16">13 Locking Hill, Lansdown,</p>
                <p class="slides-text16">Stroud, GL5 1BB</p>
                <p class="slides-text16">07545 915997</p>
                <a class="slides-text8" href="mailto:info@stroudpottery.co.uk" target="_blank">
                  <span class="slides-text16">info@stroudpottery.co.uk</span>

                <a class="slides-text8" href="https://www.stroudpottery.co.uk/" target="_blank">
                  <span class="slides-text16">stroudpottery.co.uk</span>
                </a>

              <div class="slides-text-info-block1 block-left slides-text-light" style="top: 50.5%; width: 57%; transform: translateX(4%);">
                <p class="slides-text9">The Studios is home to a collective of multi-disciplinary artists who work independently from their own spaces exploring a range of mediums; clay, glass, mosaic, woodcut printmaking, illustration and textiles. Sitting within the lower ground floor of the Centre of Science and Arts, Stroud Pottery is next door.</p>
                <p class="slides-text9">The Studios also has the added beauty of a lovingly landscaped garden that provides a great space for our artists to sketch, read or just reflect with a nice cuppa together or alone.</p>
                <p class="slides-text9">Our ethos at The Studios is to create a space that its users can feel is their own. A place for emerging artists of any age to develop and become fully immersed in their craft, with the support and connection of fellow studio users. Our artists also offer one to one tuition within their studios and workshops.</p>

                <p class="slides-text9">A collective of artists sharing skills, teaching techniques and creating mixed media artworks.</p>
                <p class="slides-text9">Zoe Kingston teaches photography and is learning printmaking techniques. She has mainly worked with collagraph so far and has been developing prints from walking drawings. She also does dry point and is learning how to cut lino.</p>
                <p class="slides-text9">Sophy Churchyard gained her degree in Fine Art at Cheltenham 2018 having previously studied architectural glass in Swansea.</p>

              </div>
              
            </div>

                <p class="slides-text9" style="margin: 0 0">A colourist and expressionist, her practice explores presence and temporality in an age of information. Described as digital photographic painting the work is vibrant vivid colour abstractions informed through extensive meditation and travel through South East Asia and India.</p>
                <p class="slides-text9" style="margin: 5% 0">Myrn Fisher is a product design secondary school teacher. She has a love for all art materials and processes and enjoys sharing her knowledge and enthusiasm with others. She sees herself as an artist, a graphic designer, a silversmith, a woodworker, a metal worker, a sculptor, a painter, and a print maker! She enjoys working collaboratively, skill sharing and playing around with mixed media.</p>

            <div class="slides-head" style="transform: translate(0%,10%)">
            <p class="slides-text15">Liberation through Substance</p>
            </div>

              <div class="slides-text-info-block1 block-left slides-text-light no-select" style="top: 21.5%; height: 70%; width: 42.5%; transform: translateX(7%);">
                <p class="slides-text16">6th-18th June</p>
                <p class="slides-text16">Mon-Fri 9:30am-4pm, Sat-Sun 10am-6pm</p>
                <p class="slides-text16">Three Storeys, Old Bristol Road, Nailsworth,</p>
                <p class="slides-text16">Gloucestershire, GL6 0JE</p>
                <p class="slides-text16">07581215120</p>
                <a class="slides-text8" href="mailto:cheryl@cherart.uk" target="_blank">
                  <span class="slides-text16">cheryl@cherart.uk</span>
                </a>
                <br>
                <a class="slides-text8" href="https://www.threestoreys.co.uk" target="_blank">
                  <span class="slides-text16">www.threestoreys.co.uk</span>
                <br>
                <p class="slides-text9">Three artists collaborate to explore the interplay between creativity, womanhood and self nurture. Botanical artist Karen Green, painter Cherryl Perrett and ceramicist Charlie Clarke share how rhythms and cycles; and learnt and inherited wisdoms inform relationships with their chosen materials, subject matter and creative processes. Throughout Karen’s study of flora, fruits, folklore and symbology, Cheryl’s release into colour, adventure and movement and Charlie’s immersion of sensuality and the chemistry between earth, water, air and fire; this exhibition communicates the rich symbiosis between female experience and artistic expression. The artists invite you to enjoy the healing power of finding a flow state when creating. Paintings, prints, sketches, pots and ceramic art for sale.</p>

              </div>
              
              <div class="slides-text-info-block1 block-middle slides-text-light no-select" style="top: 21.5%; width: 42.5%; transform: translateX(37%); height: 70%">

                </a>

                        <path class="slides-text17" style="scale:0.8;" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" d="M 31.820312 12 C 13.438312 12 12 13.439312 12 31.820312 L 12 32.179688 C 12 50.560688 13.438313 52 31.820312 52 L 32.179688 52 C 50.561688 52 52 50.560688 52 32.179688 L 52 32 C 52 13.452 50.548 12 32 12 L 31.820312 12 z M 43.994141 18 C 45.099141 17.997 45.997 18.889141 46 19.994141 C 46.003 21.099141 45.110859 21.997 44.005859 22 C 42.900859 22.003 42.003 21.110859 42 20.005859 C 41.997 18.900859 42.889141 18.003 43.994141 18 z M 31.976562 22 C 37.498562 21.987 41.987 26.454563 42 31.976562 C 42.013 37.498562 37.545437 41.987 32.023438 42 C 26.501437 42.013 22.013 37.545437 22 32.023438 C 21.987 26.501437 26.454563 22.013 31.976562 22 z M 31.986328 26 C 28.672328 26.008 25.992 28.701625 26 32.015625 C 26.008 35.328625 28.700672 38.008 32.013672 38 C 35.327672 37.992 38.008 35.299328 38 31.986328 C 37.992 28.672328 35.299328 25.992 31.986328 26 z"/>
                      </svg>                 
                    </span>
                  </span>
                </a>
                <br>
                <a class="slides-text8" href="https://www.nickgrellier.com" target="_blank">
                  <span class="slides-text16">www.nickgrellier.com</span>
                </a>
                <a class="slides-text8" href="https://www.emilylucasartwork.wordpress.com" target="_blank">
                  <span class="slides-text16">www.emilylucasartwork.wordpress.com</span>
                </a>
              </div>
              
              <div class="slides-text-info-block1 block-left slides-text-light" style="top: 50.5%; width: 57%; transform: translateX(4%);">
                <p class="slides-text9">‘houseworkwork’: collaborative drawing and installation by (both laughing) collective Nick Grellier and Emily Lucas. Over 18 months they’ve pro- duced multiple works taking diverse references from Valerie Solanas and Roland Barthes to Dolly Parton and Loyle Carner.</p>
                <p class="slides-text9">The work is grounded in drawing practice and rich research that explores, discovers, invents, solves problems and cracks jokes. The resulting exhibition presents artwork unlike their individual practices with interconnected pieces made using low value, low fi materials and objects from around the home in order to tackle the problem of emotion versus seriousness and other hierarchies both in the art world and wider society. The work is both playful and serious, celebrating difficulties and achievements in a domestic setting.</p>
              </div>
            </div>
            
            
            <div class="slides-right  no-select">
              <img class="img9" style="height: 42%; top: 0%; left: 0%;" src="/placeholder.jpg" data-src="/Grellier.N.(Both Laughing).1jpg (1).jpg">

              <img class="img9" style="height: 29%; top: 0%; left: 0%;" src="/placeholder.jpg" data-src="/Both Laughing.3.jpg">
              <p class="slides-text5" style="top: 85%; left:65%;">Housework (both laughing) Nicola Grellier and Emily Lucas</p>
            </div>

              </svg>

          </div>

            </div>
            <div class="slides-head" style="transform: translate(48%,10%)">

                <p class="slides-text16">10th-11th & 17th-18th June</p>
                <p class="slides-text16">The Nutshell Studios, Old Market,</p>
                <p class="slides-text16">Nailsworth, Glos. GL6 0DU.</p>
                <p class="slides-text16">07970 648126</p>
                <a class="slides-text8" href="mailto:viviana@rossicaffell.com" target="_blank">
                  <span class="slides-text16">viviana@rossicaffell.com</span>
                </a>
                <a class="slides-text8" href="https://www.rossicaffell.com/" target="_blank">
                  <span class="slides-text16">www.rossicaffell.com</span>
                </a>
                <p class="slides-text9">This exhibition responds to the heightened sense of nature- culture mergings in a psychologi- cal space informed by the physical experience of the land. Artists respond to the strangeness of dreamscapes, mythologies and sensing the surreal in the quotidian. Attuning to inner realms and the otherworldly, the landscape imaginaries mirror spectral fantasies. With works by Patricia Brien, Su Fahy, Michelle Grant, Nick Phillips, James Porter, Viviana Rossi-Caffell, Louise van den Muyzenberg.</p>

              </div>
              
            </div>

                <br>
                <a class="slides-text8" href="https://www.instagram.com/the_thursday_group/" target="_blank">

                <p class="slides-text9">The Thursday Group is eight local artists each with individual practices who enjoy working and learning together. The work on show reflects the range of interests within the group, from storytelling to abstract, and from landscape to portraiture. Guest tutors are invited by the group to inspire, teach and challenge and earlier this year Sue Rae (Suejrae. co.uk) led the group as they explored integrating collage into their practices.</p>

              <div class="slides-text-info-block1 block-left slides-text-light" style="top: 50.5%; width: 57%; transform: translateX(4%);">
                <p class="slides-text9">The GPC (Gloucestershire Printmaking Cooperative) is a fantastic Stroud based printmaking facility that facilitates imagemakers in the5 Valleys and beyond. Our large membership of over 100 members ranges from those just beginning their journey with ink and paper to post MA & PHD students, through to artists, illustrators and textiledesigners. We have planned a diverse exhibition for SITE OpenStudios 2023 to be displayed throughout the studios and gallery consisting of original prints that embrace different themes, scale andprocesses. The GPC ethos is to continually evolve and improve our facilities and user experience to create a professional, well-designed space for etching, lithography, fabric and paper screenprint, monoprintand photopolymer gravure. There will be printmaking demonstrations in the studios on both weekends.</p>
              </div>
            </div>

            </div>

              <div class="slides-text-info-block1 block-left slides-text-light no-select" style="top: 21.5%; height: 70%; width: 42.5%; transform: translateX(7%);">
                <p class="slides-text16">6th-18th June</p>
                <p class="slides-text16">Mon-Fri 9:30am-4pm, Sat-Sun 10am-6pm</p>
                <p class="slides-text16">The Hide Artist Retreat, Pinfarthings, Stroud, GL5 5JJ.</p>

                <a class="slides-text8" href="https://www.thehide.co/" target="_blank">
                  <span class="slides-text16">www.thehide.co</span>
                </a>
                <br>
                <a class="slides-text8" href="https://www.instagram.com/thehideartistretreat/" target="_blank">
                  <span class="slides-text16 slides-social-text">@thehideartistretreat
                    <span>
                      <svg class="slide-social-icons" style="transform: translateX(-40%);" viewbox="0 0 50 50" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" >
                        <path class="slides-text17" style="scale:0.8;" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" d="M 31.820312 12 C 13.438312 12 12 13.439312 12 31.820312 L 12 32.179688 C 12 50.560688 13.438313 52 31.820312 52 L 32.179688 52 C 50.561688 52 52 50.560688 52 32.179688 L 52 32 C 52 13.452 50.548 12 32 12 L 31.820312 12 z M 43.994141 18 C 45.099141 17.997 45.997 18.889141 46 19.994141 C 46.003 21.099141 45.110859 21.997 44.005859 22 C 42.900859 22.003 42.003 21.110859 42 20.005859 C 41.997 18.900859 42.889141 18.003 43.994141 18 z M 31.976562 22 C 37.498562 21.987 41.987 26.454563 42 31.976562 C 42.013 37.498562 37.545437 41.987 32.023438 42 C 26.501437 42.013 22.013 37.545437 22 32.023438 C 21.987 26.501437 26.454563 22.013 31.976562 22 z M 31.986328 26 C 28.672328 26.008 25.992 28.701625 26 32.015625 C 26.008 35.328625 28.700672 38.008 32.013672 38 C 35.327672 37.992 38.008 35.299328 38 31.986328 C 37.992 28.672328 35.299328 25.992 31.986328 26 z"/>
                      </svg>                 
                    </span>
                  </span>
                </a>
                <p class="slides-text9">THISS 2023 Urban/Rural presents a series of visual responses to this rural location, from these confirmed artists; Ellie Harrison, Milky, Molly Harcombe, Zed in the Clouds, working in a range of mediums to different ends and interacting with the environment and each other during the process. These four early career artists (ages 18-30yrs) bring their practices to an outside setting in an Area of Outstanding Beauty on National Trustland. A collaboratively produced event, engaging in a public facing exhibition showcasing work for an experienced, art-appreciating audience and toconnect with other young artists to build support through peer-to-peer mentoring.</p>

                <p class="slides-text9" style="font-style: italic;">There are also additional pop-up artists at THISS - check @thehideartistretreat on Instagram for more details.</p>

              </div>
              
              <div class="slides-text-info-block1 block-middle slides-text-light no-select" style="top: 21.5%; width: 42.5%; transform: translateX(37%); height: 70%">
                <p class="slides-text16">Opening night:</p>
                <p class="slides-text16">Friday 9th June 6-8pm</p>
                <p class="slides-text16">Exhibition dates:</p>
                <p class="slides-text16">Saturday 10th - Sunday 18th June</p>
                <p class="slides-text16">Wednesday-Sunday 11am-6pm</p>
                <p class="slides-text16">10 Russell St, Stroud GL5 3AB</p>
                <a class="slides-text8" href="http://www.sitefestival.org.uk/" target="_blank">
                  <span class="slides-text16">www.sitefestival.org.uk</span>
                </a>
                <p class="slides-text9">The Open Studios 2023 Taster Exhibition in the Stroud town centre offers visitors an opportunity to see one piece of work by each of the Open Studios artists, so you can plan your studio visits over the two weekends.</p>
                <p class="slides-text9">SVA has a long reputation for using empty shops in experimental ways and encouraging communities and groups to do the same, despite the challenges.</p>
                <p class="slides-text9">Find the Taster exhibition in the two empty shops on Russell Street, opposite Batemans. The exhibition is across 3 floors, and the floor surface in some rooms is uneven. We’re really grateful to all the artists, agents and volunteers who contributed to this experiment.</p>

              </div>

                  <span class="slides-text13"> 10—24 JUNE</span> </p>
